<time>1555974882374<//time><Rate>4</Rate>< Review>
Car was in the shop at American Tires down the block, so I decided to kill some time and eat Vietnamese food. I'm no culinary expert, but the two rice dishes I ordered tasted okay. Portion sizes varied--House Special had more food while the "Tender Chicken Thigh" dish was a little less. Overall interior was clean and bathrooms decent. Service was prompt and attentive. For Tustin, this is a decent restaurant if you're in the mood for Vietnamese. I didn't try any pho dishes, but heard they were very tasty.< /Review>

My husband and I have been ordering take out from this place for over a year now. We always order the same thing. 2 beef brisket ph√≥ bowls. Sometimes he orders and sometimes I order but he is always the one who picks it up. It's a 5 minute walk from our house. We continued to order frequently even throughout the pandemic. One time, i guess there was a misunderstanding between my husband and the man who placed his order over the phone. He went in to pick up our order and got 2 ph√≥ brisket bowls and upon leaving, they called him a few minutes later to ask if he was going to come pick up the order and started getting angry with him over the phone. So when he went into the restaurant to pick up our order, there was a miscommunication and instead my husband placed and paid for a new order and the takeout order was never picked up. So they thought he never came in to get our order. This was over a month ago and we have ordered at least 3 times since then. So tonight, my husband goes to place an order for the same thing we get every single time - two beef brisket bowls, and the man taking our order starts acting like he isn't going to serve us because we didn't pick up our food that one time. Well, it isn't like they ask for a name when you place your order. So my husband walking in and saying "two beef brisket bowls" and picking up fresh ones by mistake is NOT anyone's fault if it isn't the fault of the restaurant. There should be a better process of dealing with takeout orders. Needless to say, we won't be giving our patronage to this place anymore because of how rude our experience was. We went to the place next to Stater bros tonight and will continue to from now on. Personally, I don't prefer their ph√≥ and it isn't walking distance, but their service is worth the extra effort. They are always so nice and always serve us with a smile... Never threaten not to serve us food because of a misunderstanding. I would reccomend going somewhere else, especially if you are not Vietnamese as the language barrier makes it difficult for them to understand you. It's unfortunate, we would order here like 3 times a month. Never again after that kind of harassment over a simple misunderstanding. I suggest you try somewhere else, as well.<//text>

<Rating>4<//Rating>< review>
I have been here ever since I was a kid and I would say it's a really good pho restaurant. I have tried several different pho places, and if visiting Garden Grove or Westminster or any other well-known pho restaurants are too far, this is the best place to go to in Tustin. Comfort food with a welcoming service. I suggest the Pho Dac Biet for any noodle lover. The eggrolls are fairly good too. Rice and chicken plates are decent. Definitely try this place out.< /review>

<date>1622194473542</date><Rating>5<//Rating><review>Went to celebrate a friend's birthday and had the ayce lunch. Amazing quality and quantity for $23.95.   It's $28.95 at dinner.  That includes tea (ice or hot) and a small cup of delicious ice cream for dessert.  Each person gets 5 items per round, for up to 2 hours of ordering, but of course you can stay and finish long after that.   The food comes out fast, so they don't make you sit around trying to stall your food orders to save money.  It's all fresh, delicious and varied.  Really nice fried and baked items, and the raw seafood was very fresh.   Nice rolls, with a thin layer of rice as well.  Definitely quality.  It's the same food as if you were ordering a la carte. Only the carpaccio sashimi has an extra charge: 99 cents for first round,  $1.99 second round,  $2.99 third round.  We all left stuffed and very satisfied.  The only thing not great was the teriyaki chicken and beef.  Both came out only tepid, with a goopy sauce, and the beef was very tough and chewy.  Skip those.  But everything else was delicious.  For around $30/pp including tip ($5 more for dinner),  you can't beat it.   It was so great I went back 3 days later with another friend had it again!   I'll go again in another month. Thank you Zeppin!</review>< Pictures>

<Date>1501032871714</Date><rate>1< /rate><Review>07-25-2017

My girlfriend walked into this store, and received an estimate for a diagnosis on her cell phone during her lunch break. I came to the store shortly after with her phone because she had to return to work. They quoted me a different price for the diagnosis, and were not willing to negotiate on the difference with the quote.  I paid their new up charge, and they quoted me an hour.

So I ran some errands around town, and showed up shortly after an hour. The same salesman told me that the test was not done, and that it would be not too long before they knew what was going on. I was okay with that, and asked for an appropriate time to come back. They told me they had my number on file, and they would give me a call when it was done. I took off again and returned about 45 minutes later to check on the status of the phone.

A different person from the back came out which I figured was probably the tech.  He asked to see my receipt, and continued to ask why I had showed up without being called. I figured he was busy, and already upset with a separate customer. I told him that I wanted to get an appropriate time that I would be called that way I can arrange my day approipriatly, (at this time it was five till 5 pm). He became upset when I asked again for a better time estimate. Another salesman came from the back, and tried to tell me that I need to leave so they can do their job. I told the third employee my conversation with second employee was not delaying the computer that was plugged into my phone. I restated all I wanted was an estimated time. Both employees went to the back after saying they were just going to hand me my broken phone.

The original person I spoke with came from the back, and he told me very politely that the tests were not done yet. He explained it would be a little while before they called me. I was okay with that, and went to exit the store when the other two walked out of the back. The second employee had my girlfriends phone in hand.

The second employee handed me the phone, and stated here's your phone, goodbye. I asked if it was fixed, and he said "No you can leave my store, I'm not touching your phone anymore." I asked for my refund, and he said "no you paid for it and I don't like the way you spoke with me." I told him I paid for a service that wasn't fulfilled. He told me he did not care, and he was not fixing the phone.

I spent a total of almost 2 hours waiting to receive a service that I did not get.  The second employee that spoke with me also identified himself as "Jagpreet, the owner of the store."

<rating>5<//rating><user_id>105536843127229431886</user_id><time>1620620375352</time><Text>Excellent Mexican cocktail and food establishment in downtown Palo Alto. Recently opened. We were impressed by the high quality of the cocktails and food, the uniqueness in the menu items, and the excellent customer service that knew "everything" about the menu. Prices can be a little steep, but that's California. I would compare this place to Milagros in Redwood City, but this San Augus has much better drinks and food. If you're looking for a high quality restaurant experience and amazing craft cocktails, I highly recommend this place. Details to follow:

[The Drinks]
Starting with the best part, the drinks were excellent here. They have a wide variety of cocktails I have never tried anywhere else. Most of them are named after sayings or phrases in Spanish. They don't taste like they have a bunch of fillers and artificial flavors. The drinks tasted real with quality ingredients and careful thought into the mix. We tried about 5 and couldn't decide which one was our favorite. Could use just a tad more alcohol but they were balanced, and we will absolutely be returning just to get drinks one day.

[The Food]
We were really impressed by the food too. The presentation of the food and the quality was what we expected given the price. We got Quesabarria tacos which were excellent. They have a variety of different offerings which are well described and seems to be high quality. We were absolutely impressed.

[The Location]
The restaurant is located near University Ave in downtown Palo Alto. It's in a nice spot near Caltrain, off the beaten path so there's plenty of parking. It's safe, well lit, and has outdoor seating! The restaurant looks super clean and well maintained!<//Text>< Gmap_id>

< review>
The torta cubano was absolutely delicious. Loved the flavor profile and have deep depth and complexity. Good mix of meats and veggies with a lovely toasted bread. Sauce tied everything together. Price was good and the portion sizes are good too.

The esquites on the other hand was a salted creamy corn and cotija cheese mix. Portion size is a bit lacking IMO and the flavor was interesting but a bit over seasoned and one dimensional.< /review>

<Name>Erik Ortiz<//Name><GmapID>0x80dc9dedb2c2ee09:0x35519d575a92440c<//GmapID><Date>1480523990110<//Date><pictures>None< /pictures><text>I have been reading through these comments and it seems like 80% of the comments are related to the contract/billing. 20% is about the fact that its not like Menifee 24/7.

Of course its not like the old gym. NEW OWNERS! NEW PROCEDURES! Give them time everything will come around.

Like any contract, read it please before you sign! You have money coming out of your bank account, why would you not want to read it! Your not going to sign your name on the dotted line before you buy a car. So why would you do it for a gym membership! C'mon!

Its simple, if you want to pay a dollar to join and $10.00 a month after that  you are locked on to a year contract. So pay a little extra and go with the month to month option that is explained to you during the sign up.

Okay, now about the gym.
-The staff that i deal with are good to go. Young kids but they know the regulars. They clean and re-rack weights do what they have to do for the customers.
-The gym equipment is all in really good shape. If something breaks they have it fixed fairly quickly.

-The Men's locker room/bathroom is not really maintained. Its always dirty and out of paper towels and toilet paper. Showers smell and curtains defiantly need to be replaced. But what can i say. Its a bathroom. Toilets flush and showers work. I am good personally, its just my opinion.

-The vibe is great. This gym is defiantly a gym that everyone is welcome at. No judgmental people. (During the times that i am their i cant speak for the other 22 1/2 hours i am not their.

- The trainers defiantly don't look or act like trainers hard for me to see any confidence in their abilities. They kind of look like individuals that got their certificate and found a job for personal training. Once again my opinion. I have never dealt with them personally this opinion is based of perception. I wouldn't pay for it.

-I haven't done any of the classes so couldn't comment on those.

-i don't use the pool, basketball court or racket ball court so couldn't comment on those.

-The cardio equipment is all in really good shape. They have everything you will need. Even a movie cardio room for those days you just want to come in and keep your mind off your cardio session with something other then your music.

Things that I would like to see change. The music that plays on the loud speakers is really bad. Yes i can use my headphones and listen to my own music but i really don't like to work out with headphones in. I like to focus on my mind muscle connection. The music is my only complaint.

Once again, these are my opinions. I really like it here and would defiantly recommend this gym to all my peer's. I am really excited to see the future of this gym when everything is squared away!

I hope this helps people out with there choice.

Thank you!< /text><rating>5< /rating>< user>

111142428228057552076< /user_id>
<username>Don Downing</username><date>1366750930753<//date><Rate>4</Rate>< review>
Set off the street in a plain industrial park style area, the San Diego Volleyball Club is a large facility with 4 full courts, trampoline area, gymnastics spring floor, and weight training area.

We enrolled in a starter skills class for our 10yo girl.  The class is about 25 girls and there is one main instructor with a handful of helper instructors.  The instruction is fun, friendly, and focused on building basic ball handling skills for the girls.  During our class the girls will run between all 4 courts, hitting, scooping up their ball, then running to the next station.

There is plenty of parking in front and around the building, although the white lines have long faded so I'm never sure if I'm parked right.  The facility is clean, ample parent seating in various areas, a snack bar that is probably only open during tournements, and *free WIFI.*   Bathrooms are large and clean.  Each volleyball court is surrounded with netting so no stray balls.

Word from other parents is that the instructors will let us know when our girl has achieved enough skills to try out for the team.

Of note, there is no real "front desk" area with someone there watching over things or the front door.  But I'm always eyeballs-on my kids anyway.< /review>
